
----  Linked server : IT13
sp_addlinkedserver 'IT13','SQL Server'
go
sp_addlinkedsrvlogin 'IT13','false',null,'repl_user',<enter password here>
go
sp_serveroption 'IT13','collation compatible','off'
go
sp_serveroption 'IT13','data access','on'
go
sp_serveroption 'IT13','rpc','on'
go
sp_serveroption 'IT13','rpc out','on'
go
sp_serveroption 'IT13','use remote collation','off'
go
sp_serveroption 'IT13','collation name',null
go
sp_serveroption 'IT13','connect timeout',0
go
sp_serveroption 'IT13','query timeout','0'
go

-- Options for provider : SQLOLEDB

go

go
exec master..xp_regwrite 'HKEY_LOCAL_MACHINE','SOFTWARE\Microsoft\MSSQLServer\Providers\SQLOLEDB','LevelZeroOnly','REG_DWORD',1
go
exec master..xp_regwrite 'HKEY_LOCAL_MACHINE','SOFTWARE\Microsoft\MSSQLServer\Providers\SQLOLEDB','AllowInProcess','REG_DWORD',1
go
exec master..xp_regwrite 'HKEY_LOCAL_MACHINE','SOFTWARE\Microsoft\MSSQLServer\Providers\SQLOLEDB','NonTransactedUpdates','REG_DWORD',1
go
exec master..xp_regwrite 'HKEY_LOCAL_MACHINE','SOFTWARE\Microsoft\MSSQLServer\Providers\SQLOLEDB','IndexAsAccessPath','REG_DWORD',1
go
